Jul 14 - Jul 20, 2025

Plugins / superconsole - Windows-only

  • rtm-reminder (‚≠ê0) - Displays urgent Remember The Milk tasks after each command execution. Clean, non-intrusive, and terminal-only.
  • sshinfo (‚≠ê0) - displays resolved SSH connection details (like the final hostname, port, user, and proxies) before connecting. This is useful for verifying your SSH configuration, especially when dealing with complex setups involving aliases, proxies, or multiple configuration files.
  • system-update (‚≠ê0) - A smart, efficient system update plugin for oh-my-zsh that handles APT packages, Conda environments, and pip installations with intelligent caching to minimize update times.

Completions / superconsole - Windows-only

  • codex (‚≠ê0) - Vibe-coded tab completion for OpenAI's codex (‚≠ê31k) tool. Generates completions in the background so it doesn't slow down shell startup.

Themes / superconsole - Windows-only

  • larn (‚≠ê1) - A clean and customizable oh my zsh theme with Git integration, designed for dark terminals. It features a colorful prompt with decorators for git branch and status indicators, current directory and distinct ls colors for files and directories.
  • serenity (‚≠ê0) - Minimalist theme which displays essential context info in soft-colored boxes above the command line, using Unicode separators to stay clean yet expressive. Includes decorators for root status, username, hostname, host IP address, git status and current directory.

Jul 07 - Jul 13, 2025

awesome-lazy-zsh

  • Plugin Management: Install and manage plugins easily.
  • Theme Customization: Apply a variety of Zsh themes.
  • Backup and Restore: Safeguard your .zshrc configurations.
  • Interactive CLI: User-friendly setup options.
  • Dependency Management: Automatically checks for Git, Node.js, and Homebrew.

Plugins / superconsole - Windows-only

  • flutter-zsh-shortcuts (‚≠ê0) - Adds clean aliases for flutter commands.
  • git-plugin-cheatsheet (‚≠ê0) - Displays the aliases and functions available from the git oh-my-zsh plugin.
  • proj-jumper (‚≠ê0) - A lightweight ZSH plugin that lets you jump straight into any project folder under a single development root -- perfect when that root lives on a removable drive.

Completions / superconsole - Windows-only

  • justfile (‚≠ê0) - Adds tab completions for just (‚≠ê26k).
  • tio (‚≠ê0) - Add tab completions for tio

Themes / superconsole - Windows-only

  • dalailahner (‚≠ê0) - Minimalist theme with decorators for git status, for VCS status (based on Bart Trojanowski's zsh prompt), username and current directory. Based on Steve Losh's Prose (‚≠ê350) theme.
  • ykali (‚≠ê2) - Prints a modifiable banner for each new ZSH session. Includes decorators for username, hostname, current directory, wlan0 IP and git information.

Jun 30 - Jul 06, 2025

Plugins / superconsole - Windows-only

  • env-secrets (‚≠ê0) - Automatically retrieves secrets from secure storage backends and exports them as environment variables during shell initialization. This eliminates the need to store sensitive information in plain text configuration files. Works with pass and the macOS keychain.
  • sops-crypt (‚≠ê1) - Plugin for Mozilla SOPS that provides one-click encryption and decryption of files in the current directory and subdirectories.
  • zshcp (‚≠ê1) - A lightweight and intuitive clipboard management plugin for Zsh that enhances your command-line workflow with easy copy-paste operations.
  • zwirl (‚≠ê0) - Adds aliases for git and eza.

Themes / superconsole - Windows-only

  • base (‚≠ê2) - A minimal and functional ZSH theme designed for developers and sysadmins who frequently work on remote servers, VPS, or VPNs. Includes decorators for your public IP address, git status and current directory.
  • henzilla (‚≠ê0) - Inspired bygozilla (‚≠ê180k). Includes decorator for git status.
  • kindahv (‚≠ê3) - A clean ZSH theme with command execution time tracking.
  • moonlight (‚≠ê0) - Dark lunar aesthetic with celestial tokens for git status.Heavily inspired by the daivasmara (‚≠ê86) theme.
  • simple-zsh-catppuccin (‚≠ê0) - Based on the Catppuccin Mocha color scheme, adapted from the Dracula (‚≠ê282) theme foundation. This theme features a simple and functional prompt with support for git status, time display, context, and directory information, enhanced with hex color support discovered by ezswan.
  • taw-ys-venv (‚≠ê1) - Two-line prompt with decorators for username, current directory, git information and current Python venv. Based on AzarAI-TOP/taw-ys-zsh-theme (‚≠ê1).

Jun 16 - Jun 22, 2025

Plugins / superconsole - Windows-only

  • journal (‚≠ê2) - Lets you attach notes to shell commands you have run. Handy for remembering what a oneliner was actually doing when you look back at it later.
  • warrior (‚≠ê0) - Uses a local large language model (Ollama) to translate natural-language into ZSH commands.

Completions / superconsole - Windows-only

  • alembic (‚≠ê1) - Adds completions for Alembic, the database migration tool for SQLAlchemy. Includes helper functions for faster workflow, command aliases and status overview functions.
  • nestcli (‚≠ê1) - Tab completion for the Nest.js CLI (‚≠ê2.1k).

Themes / superconsole - Windows-only

  • gallium (‚≠ê0) - Minimal theme inspired by gal (‚≠ê3) and gallois (‚≠ê180k). Includes decorators for username@host, current directory and git status.
  • musy (‚≠ê0) - Inspured by muse theme. Includes git status decorations.
  • suprima-asra (‚≠ê0) - A feature-rich minimal theme inspired by Ultima (‚≠ê105). Includes decorators for battery status, multi-VCS (git, hg and svn), whether or not it's an ssh connection, exit status of last command, command timing, current time, username@host, active python venv, node version, docker-compose detection and project context awareness.

Jun 09 - Jun 15, 2025

Prerequisites

  • More Nerd Fonts - Another site to download Nerd Fonts.

Themes / superconsole - Windows-only

  • appa (‚≠ê0) - A tidy little theme based on omz's refined (‚≠ê180k). Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k).
  • bahman (‚≠ê1) - Requires Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k). Has git status decorator.
  • blaze (‚≠ê32) - Visually similar to powerline. Requires make and g++. Works best with your terminal set to use a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k). Includes decorators for current directory, execution time of last command, exit status of last command, git status information, date, time, username and host. Can be extended with custom segments.
  • boban (‚≠ê1) - A powerline-style file based on Agnoster (‚≠ê4.1k). Includes decorators for user@hostname, git status, current working directory, python venv, AWS profile, $KUBECONFIG, the terraform workspace and the exit status of the last command run. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k) for symbols to render properly.
  • candy-light - Light version of the candy theme.
  • checkmate (‚≠ê1) - Decorated with chess pieces. Includes decorators for python venv, current directory, git status and whether you're running as root. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k).
  • droolmaw (‚≠ê0) - Configurable prompt that resembles Powerline (‚≠ê15k). Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k). Includes decorators for username, current directory, current directory path, datetime, git author, git status, mise language version and a configurable message based on the exit status of the last command run.
  • hietan (‚≠ê1) - Includes decorators for current directory, date & time, git status and the exit value of the last command run. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k).
  • ichirei (‚≠ê0) - Colorful. Includes decorators for git status, time & current directory. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k).
  • nerdp (‚≠ê3) - Nerd powerline-style prompt. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k). Includes decorators for git status, username@hostname, current directory, Python virtualenv, filesystem usage check, 1 minute CPU load, available memory and the time.
  • nerdps1 (‚≠ê13) - Reminiscent of powerline. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k). Includes decorators for user@hostname, git information, truncated current directory, python virtualenv, exit status of last command run and the time.
  • nidoranarion - Colorful, shows git status decorations.
  • ninik (‚≠ê3) - Inspired by agnoster (‚≠ê4.1k) and ubunly (‚≠ê31). Includes decorators for OS, current directory, python virtualenv and git status. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k) or Powerline-patched font.
  • paramour (‚≠ê1) - Simple and clean, has decorators for git status, username, time, current directory and username. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k) in your terminal.
  • thayne (‚≠ê1) - Includes decorators for exit status of last command, time to run if > 1 second, current time, current directory and git status. Requires a Nerd Font (‚≠ê59k).

May 26 - Jun 01, 2025

Usepkg

  • fetch & load plugin(s) with declared methods
  • list, check, reload, update & remove plugin(s) with commands
  • zsh
  • gnu coreutils
  • git (optional, if you want to clone git repositories from internet)
  • curl (optional, if you want to fetch a script file by url)
  • extremely simple and light, but enough to use.
  • compared to similar packages like zplug, it has a much simpler configuration grammar.

ZSH Tools / superconsole - Windows-only

  • completion-generators (‚≠ê1) - Has a table of tool names and the commands for outputting completion scripts for those tools. On every load, will check that table and run the completion command for every tool found in your $PATH and save its output to a file _. If the path of this repo is in $fpath, completions will work immediately.

Jun 24 - Jun 30, 2024

x-cmd

  • Wrappers for Common Commands (e.g., cd, ip, ps, tar, apt, brew): These wrapped commands are more intelligent and easier to use compared to the native commands.
  • Lightweight Package Management Tool: We have implemented a lightweight package management tool using shell and awk. Through it, you can quickly obtain most common software tools, such as jq, 7za, bat, nvim, python, node, go, etc.
  • CLI for Useful Websites (e.g., github.com, cht.sh): We have wrapped their APIs using shell and awk for daily use and to obtain corresponding services in scripts.
  • AI Tools: We provide CLIs for ChatGPT, Gemini, Jina.ai, etc., and have wrapped corresponding shortcut commands for different application scenarios, such as @gemini for chatting with Gemini AI and @zh for using AI to translate specified content or command results.

Plugins / superconsole - Windows-only

  • caniuse (‚≠ê19) - Add Can I Use support to ZSH.
  • check-deps (‚≠ê3) - Helper for ZSH plugins that allows them to show how to install any missing dependencies. Works on Debian (and derivatives like Ubuntu), Arch and its derivatives, Node.js and ZSH plugins if you are using the zpm (‚≠ê371) framework.
  • docker-aliases (‚≠ê8) - Docker aliases for everyday use.
  • docker-compose (‚≠ê50) - Show docker container status in your prompt.
  • gitgo (‚≠ê11) - Open a GitHub/GitLab repository in your browser from the command line (macOS only).
  • github-folders (‚≠ê0) - Organizes your GitHub checkouts for you.
  • hebzsh (‚≠ê1) - If a command is not found as typed in Hebrew, translates the command as if it was typed on a keyboard with a US English layout and tries again.
  • history-enquirer (‚≠ê97) - Enhances history search with more interaction and a multiline selection menu. Requires Node.js.
  • incsearch (‚≠ê5) - Friendlier vim mode for ZSH. Moves cursor with incremental search within current line.
  • lux (‚≠ê35) - ZSH plugin to toggle the light & dark modes of macOS, iTerm 2, Visual Studio Code and other items and applications via the lux command. Highly customizable: included items can be configured by defining variables. Highly extensible: items can be added by defining functions. Includes a macos_is_dark helper function to determine if the macOS dark mode is active for use in theming.
  • node (‚≠ê5) - Srijan Shetty's Node.js plugin for ZSH with caching of nvm completions and autoloading of nvm if present.
  • php-version-switcher (‚≠ê2) - Changes php versions if a .php-version file is found.
  • pr-node (‚≠ê0) - Sets an environment variable which can be used to display Node.js information in a custom prompt.
  • project (gko) (‚≠ê20) - Create node/python/ruby projects both locally and on GitHub (private or public repository).
  • shelf (‚≠ê1) - Utility which can be used to bookmark and access directly any file using mnemonics.
  • vcshr (‚≠ê0) - Help vcsh users require GitHub repositories using vcsh for auto-installation in ~/.zshrc, etc.
  • vi-mode (nyquase) (‚≠ê32) - Add extra vi-like functionality.
  • volta (cowboyd) (‚≠ê9) - Seamlessly install and configure the Volta Node.js toolchain manager.
  • web-search (anant-mishra1729) (‚≠ê4) - Adds aliases for searching with Google, Bing, Wiki, YouTube, Yahoo, Duck Duck Go, GitHub, Stack Overflow and other services straight from the command line.
  • zautoload (‚≠ê4) - Autoloader for ZSH config files.
  • zce (‚≠ê65) - Vim's EasyMotion / Emacs's ace-jump-mode for ZSH.
  • zero (‚≠ê16) - Zero is both a plugin and a theme. See the GitHub page for installation details. Includes git and hg status decorators.
  • znvm (‚≠ê1) - A Node.js version manager for ZSH similar to nvm.sh (‚≠ê86k) but faster.

zshing

Prerequisites

  • Cascadia Code (‚≠ê27k) - Microsoft's Cascadia Code
  • Fira Mono (‚≠ê5.1k) - Mozilla's Fira type family.
  • Hack - Another Powerline-compatible font designed for source code and terminal usage.
  • Input Mono - A family of fonts designed specifically for code. It offers both monospaced and proportional fonts and includes Powerline glyphs.
  • Monoid - Monoid is customizable and optimized for coding with bitmap-like sharpness at 15px line-height even on low res displays.
  • Mononoki - Mononoki is a typeface by Matthias Tellen, created to enhance code formatting.
  • Nerd fonts (‚≠ê59k) - A collection of over 20 patched fonts (over 1,700 variations) & the fontforge font patcher python script for Powerline, devicons, and vim-devicons: includes Droid Sans, Meslo, AnonymousPro, ProFont, Inconsolta, and many more. These can be installed with brew - do brew tap homebrew/cask-fonts && brew install --cask fontname
  • Spacemono (‚≠ê401) - Google's new original monospace display typeface family.
  • Victor Mono - Victor Mono is a free programming font with semi-connected cursive italics, symbol ligatures (!=, ->>, =>, ===, <=, >=, ++) and Latin, Cyrillic and Greek characters.

ZSH on Windows / superconsole - Windows-only

  • ConEmu/zsh out-of-the-box configured to restore previously opened tabs and shell working directories after ConEmu restart
  • Choose between clean and inherited environment when starting new SuperConsole sessions
  • Custom colorful scheme, colorful output for various commands
  • MSYS2 included, zsh and necessary software preinstalled, uses zsh-grml-config
  • Uses Antigen (‚≠ê8.2k) for ZSH theme and config management
  • Enabled number of ZSH plugins to activate completion, highlighting and history for most comfortable use
  • Git-for-Windows repo with proper git and git lfs support for MSYS2 environment is configured, git client already installed.
  • ssh-agent for git works out-of-box, add your keys to ConEmu/msys64/ConEmu/msys64/home/user/.ssh dir
  • Non-blocking ZSH prompt status updates thanks to agkozak-zsh-prompt (‚≠ê313)
  • Command-not-found handler customized for MSYS2 suggests what package to install
  • Sets up nano as main editor, enables nano syntax highlighting
  • Custom helper scripts added to ConEmu/msys64/3rdparty

  • gocilla (‚≠ê0) - Theme for iTerm 2 and ZSH. Uncludes git status, user@host, path and date decorators.
  • grs (‚≠ê0) - Includes git status, user id and working directory decorators.
  • hackersaurus (‚≠ê11) - A theme with git status and exit code of last command run decorators embedded in the prompt. Related to powerlevel9k (‚≠ê13k).
  • iay (‚≠ê7) - A {ba,z}sh prompt written in Rust. Includes decorations for the current directory and git status.
  • jcl (‚≠ê2) - Loosely based on the ys theme.
  • jovial (‚≠ê522) - Shows decorators for host, user, path, development environment, git branch, and which python venv is active.
  • lambda (cdimascio) (‚≠ê68) - Inspired by the lambda (‚≠ê180k) theme. Includes git status decorations.
  • minimal (glsorre) (‚≠ê0) - A minimal asynchronous ZSH theme optimized for use with the Fira Code (‚≠ê79k) font and the Solarized Light terminal theme.
  • ortiz (guezwhoz) (‚≠ê105) - Simplified fork of eriner (‚≠ê22) with git status, kubectl context and elapsed time decorations.
  • powerline-pills (‚≠ê20) - Written in Ruby, uses powerline characters to simulate pills with useful information.
  • pure-agnoster (‚≠ê4) - Mashup of pure (‚≠ê14k) and agnoster. Has git decorations and works well with both dark and light terminal backgrounds.
  • purity (‚≠ê14) - Inspired by the robbyrussell (‚≠ê180k) theme and the pure (‚≠ê14k) prompt.
  • quewui (‚≠ê1) - Simple and clean theme optimized for dark terminal themes. Includes decorations for the current time, user, directory and git status.
  • remolueoend (‚≠ê0) - Based on Agnoster (‚≠ê4.1k), using emojis for tracking git context. Only works with Prezto (‚≠ê14k).
  • rzh (‚≠ê2) - Theme with git states indicated by emojis.
  • samshell (‚≠ê1) - A minimalist ZSH theme with git, kubernetes and python virtualenv decorations.
  • schminitz-v2 (‚≠ê0) - Shows decorators for git status, user@host information, the exit status of last command, and whether running as root.
  • senpai (‚≠ê11) - Clean prompt theme for Devops. Includes decorators for git status, the kubernetes context, AWS profile, GCP project and Azure active cloud.
  • seti_UX (‚≠ê2) - A simple oh-my-zsh-compatible theme with a corresponding iTerm 2 color scheme.
  • shellder (‚≠ê296) - Minimal theme with a git branch decorator. Requires a Powerline-compatible font.
  • shuttle (‚≠ê0) - Written in golang. Has decorators for OS, user, current directory, and the exit code of the last command run.
  • simple (rkitover) (‚≠ê2) - A simple, lightweight, and nice looking prompt that runs quickly even in very slow shells like MSYS2, Cygwin and WSL. It shows decorations for the short name of the current environment (distribution, OS, etc.) the git branch when in a git checkout, as well as the last command exit status (green checkmark for success and red X mark for non-zero exit).
  • spaceship (‚≠ê20k) - Theme with git, nvm, rvm/rbenv/chruby, python, ssh and other useful status decorators.
  • steef (danihodovic) (‚≠ê4) - Oh-my-zsh steeef theme as a standalone repository. The purpose behind this repo is avoid having a dependency on oh-my-zsh when using the steeef theme. ZSH plugin managers such as Antibody can use the theme without having to use oh-my-zsh.
  • tsotra (‚≠ê2) - Minimalist theme, includes decorators for git status, k8s context, and rvm status.
  • ultimate (‚≠ê12) - Minimalist theme with decorators for git status, vim mode indicator and shortened path.
  • vinhnx (‚≠ê7) - Modified from mgutz (‚≠ê180k). Looks great when using with a Solarized (‚≠ê16k) color scheme.
  • xxf - Shows the current git commit's shortened hash and message.

Apr 25 - May 01, 2022

miniplug

  • No crashes or double plugin loading when re-sourcing .zshrc
  • Unlike other frameworks, Miniplug does not pollute your $PATH

zplug

  • Unlike antigen (‚≠ê8.2k), no ZSH plugin files (*.plugin.zsh) are required

zpm

  • zpm runs on Linux, macOS, FreeBSD and Android.
  • zpm plugins are compatible with oh-my-zsh.

zshing

  • Keep track of and configure your plugins right in the .zshrc
  • Run the above actions in a single command

zgenom

  • zsh-quickstart-kit (‚≠ê841) - A simple quickstart for using ZSH with zgenom (‚≠ê393). This automatically configures ZSH to use zgenom (‚≠ê393) to load a curated (but easily customizable) collection of plugins and periodically automatically update itself, the plugins, and the quickstart kit itself.

Feb 14 - Feb 20, 2022

Frameworks

  • pm-perf-test (‚≠ê4) - Tooling for running performance tests on multiple ZSH frameworks.

miniplug

  • Only does the bare minimum for managing plugins

sheldon

  • Can manage
    • Any git repository.
      • Branch/tag/commit support.
      • Extra support for GitHub repositories.
      • Extra support for Gists.
    • Arbitrary remote files, simply specify the URL.
    • Local plugins, simply specify the directory path.
  • Highly configurable install methods using handlebars templating.
  • Super-fast parallel installation.
  • Configuration file using TOML (‚≠ê20k) syntax.
  • Uses a lock file for much faster loading of plugins.

zpm

  • Dependencies between packages
  • Fastest plugin manager (Really, after the first run, zpm will not be used at all)
  • Support for async loading

zshing

  • Install ZSH plugins
  • Update ZSH plugins
  • Search by name all available ZSH Plugins
  • Clean unused plugins up

zulu

  • Easily manage your shell environment without editing files.
  • Create aliases, functions and environment variables, and have them available to you at the next shell startup.
  • Add and remove directories from $path, $fpath and $cdpath with simple commands.
  • Install packages, plugins and themes easily, and have them available to you immediately.

zinit

  • ZPWR (‚≠ê206) - An extremely powerful custom terminal environment built on top of Zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) for maximum speed. A full terminal configuration framework including zsh, tmux, fzf, vim and spacemacs configurations. It includes:

  • Powerline patched font collection (‚≠ê26k) - A collection of a dozen or so fonts patched to include powerline gylphs.

  • Hack - Another Powerline-compatible font designed specifically for source code.
  • Input Mono - A family of fonts designed specifically for code. It offers both monospaced and proportional fonts and includes powerline glyphs.
  • Monoid - Monoid is customizable and optimized for coding with bitmap-like sharpness at 15px line-height even on low res displays.
  • Nerd Fonts (‚≠ê59k) - Collection of over 20 patched fonts (over 2,000 variations) & FontForge font patcher python script for Powerline, Font Awesome, Octicons, Devicons, and Vim Devicons. Includes: Droid Sans, Meslo, Source Code, AnonymousPro, Hack, ProFont, Inconsolata, and many more.
  • Terminus - TTF version of Terminus that includes powerline glyphs.

  • Why ZSH is Cooler than your Shell - slideshare presentation.

  • ZSH Pony (‚≠ê182) - Covers customizing ZSH without a framework.
  • ZSH tips by Christian Schneider - An exhaustive list of ZSH tips by Christian Schneider.

  • 256color (‚≠ê145) - Enhances the terminal environment with 256 colors. It looks at the chosen TERM environment variable and sees if there is respective ncurses' terminfo with 256 colors available. The result is a multicolor terminal, if available.

Allows you to run multiple asynchronous jobs, enforce unique jobs (multiple instances of the same job will not run), flush all currently running jobs and create multiple workers (each with their own jobs).

  • you-should-use (‚≠ê1.7k) - ZSH plugin that reminds you to use those aliases you defined.
  • youtube-dl-aliases (‚≠ê7) - Adds yt aliases to download videos from YouTube.
  • youtube-dl (‚≠ê2) - Simple plugin for youtube-dl.
  • z.lua (‚≠ê3.1k) - A command line tool which helps you navigate faster by learning your habits. An alternative to z.sh (‚≠ê17k) with Windows and posix shells support and various improvements. 10x faster than fasd and autojump, 3x faster than z.sh (‚≠ê17k).
  • zabb (‚≠ê41) - zabb is a command that tries to figure out the shortest memorable abbreviation of a directory that is usable by z (‚≠ê28k) to unambiguously jump to that directory.
  • zabrze (‚≠ê42) - A ZSH abbreviation expansion plugin.
  • zaw (‚≠ê577) - ZSH anything.el-like widget.
  • zcolors (‚≠ê81) - Uses your $LS_COLORS to generate a coherent theme for Git and your Zsh prompt, completions and ZSH syntax highlighting (‚≠ê21k).
  • zconvey (‚≠ê3) - Adds ability to send commands to other ZSH sessions, you can use this to cd $PWD on all active ZSH sessions, for example.
  • zed (‚≠ê7) - A simple wrapper for z (‚≠ê17k) to install it via a ZSH plugin.
  • zeno (‚≠ê179) - Fuzzy completion and utility plugin powered by Deno.
  • zflai (‚≠ê3) - A fast logging framework for ZSH.
  • zfzf (‚≠ê25) - A fzf-powered file picker for ZSH which allows you to quickly navigate the directory hierarchy.
  • zhooks (‚≠ê66) - Displays the contents of any ZSH hook arrays and the code of any hook functions that have been defined. Useful for debugging.
  • zinfo_line (‚≠ê1) - Makes more information available to ZSH themes.
  • zinit-annex-bin-gem-node (‚≠ê7) - zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) extension that exposes binaries without altering $PATH, installs Ruby gems and Node modules and easily exposes their binaries, and updates the gems and modules when the associated plugin or snippet is updated.
  • zinit-annex-default-ice (‚≠ê3) - Allows user to define ices active for multiple zinit commands.
  • zinit-annex-man (‚≠ê6) - Zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) extension that generates man pages for all plugins and snippets
  • zinit-annex-meta-plugins (‚≠ê7) - Install groups of plugins with a single label (zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) only).
  • zinit-annex-patch-dl (‚≠ê3) - zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) extension that downloads files and applies patches through the provided dl and patch zinit ices.
  • zinit-annex-readurl (‚≠ê7) - Adds function to automatically download the newest version of a file to which URL is hosted on a webpage.
  • zinit-annex-rust (‚≠ê6) - zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) extension that that installs rust and cargo packages inside plugin directories.
  • zinit-annex-test (‚≠ê0) - zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) extension that runs tests (via make test, for example) ‚Äì if it finds any of them ‚Äì after installing and updating a plugin or snippet.
  • zinit-annex-unscope (‚≠ê2) - Allows installing plugins for zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) without specifying the user name by querying the Github API.
  • zinit-console (‚≠ê14) - A semigraphical (curses) consolette for the zinit (‚≠ê3.8k) plugin manager.
  • zinsults (‚≠ê16) - Prints insults if a command fails.
  • zjump (‚≠ê11) - Simplify ZSH directory navigation; jump to already visited, parent or sub folders.
  • zlitefetch (‚≠ê6) - Lightweight system information plugin.
  • zoxide (‚≠ê28k) - A fast alternative to cd that learns your habits.
  • zsh-select (‚≠ê10) - Displays a selection list. It is similar to selecta, but uses the curses library to do display, and when compared to fzf (‚≠ê72k), the main difference is approximate matching instead of fuzzy matching.
  • zsh-z (agkozak) (‚≠ê2.2k) - Jump quickly to directories that you have visited "frecently." A native ZSH port of z.sh - without awk, sed, sort, or date.
  • zsh-z (ptavares) (‚≠ê0) - Installs and loads z.
  • zshrc (‚≠ê5) - Load local .zshrc files from your project scopes.
  • zsnapac (‚≠ê2) - Plugin for taking ZFS pre/post upgrade snapshots on Arch Linux.
  • zsnapshot (‚≠ê3) - Adds command to dump the current ZSH state into a file, for later restoration by sourcing the snapshot file.
  • ztouch (‚≠ê3) - Adds touchbar controls for recent history commands, directory stack, cycling between modes and user-mappable commands to the touchbar on macOS.
  • ztrace (‚≠ê8) - Catches output of commands, allows to reuse that output, glue it with history content.
  • zui (‚≠ê13) - ZSH User Interface library ‚Äì CGI+DHTML-like rapid TUI application development with ZSH.)

Themes / superconsole - Windows-only

  • 0i0 (‚≠ê15) - Optimized for dark terminal windows, uses nerdfont git status decorations.
  • 14degree (‚≠ê2) - Includes git, virtualenv and rvm status decorations.
  • abbr (theme) (‚≠ê2) - Displays an abbreviated version of the current directory path, shows the Python virtualenv, Rust version, git status, and the exit code of last command. Works well on dark backgrounds by default but colors can be easily customized.
  • adlee (‚≠ê0) - macOS theme, requires a Powerline-compatible font.

  • aftermath (‚≠ê1) - Get a nice summary line after each command you run in your shell.
  • agitnoster (‚≠ê7) - Based on agnoster theme included in Oh My Zsh (‚≠ê180k) and bash-git-prompt (‚≠ê6.8k). Shows detailed information about git status.
  • agkozak (‚≠ê313) - Uses three asynchronous methods to keep the ZSH prompt responsive while displaying the git status and indicators of SSH connection, exit codes, and vi mode, along with an abbreviated, PROMPT_DIRTRIM-style path. Very customizable. Asynchronous even on Cygwin and MSYS2.
  • agnoster-gentoo (‚≠ê1) - A Gentoo flavored version of the Agnoster ZSH Theme (‚≠ê4.1k) that includes user@hostname and git status decorations. Works better with a unicode font.

  • agnoster-repopath (‚≠ê2) - Based on Agnoster (‚≠ê4.1k) and Passion (‚≠ê317) themes. Includes git and mercurial status, current time and time the last command took decorations in the prompt.
  • agnoster-timestamp-newline (‚≠ê6) - Agnoster variant with timestamp and newline added.

  • agnosterzak (‚≠ê393) - Based on Agnoster, shows battery life, date & time, git status, current directory and user & host information.

  • alpharized (‚≠ê11) - Optimized to work with solarized dark terminals. It's a modified version of the avit theme (‚≠ê180k).

  • tvline (‚≠ê2) - Derived from the agnoster theme, adds powerline font enhancements.
  • twilight (‚≠ê2) - Minimalist, but includes last command exit status, git status and user@hostname decorations.
  • type0 (‚≠ê0) - Inspired by classyTouch (‚≠ê53) by yarisgutierrez. Includes git decorations.
  • typewritten (‚≠ê932) - Minimal and informative theme that leaves room for what's important. Does asynchronous git decoration updates for speed.
  • ubunly (‚≠ê31) - Mimics the Kali Linux console. Note - this theme also rebinds a lot of keys and sets a bunch of ZSH options that themes should leave alone.
  • ubuntu-ish (‚≠ê0) - Mimics the default Debian/Ubuntu bash prompt.
  • ubuntu-with-vitamins (‚≠ê0) - Mimics the default Ubuntu prompt, but with git decorations.
  • ubuntu (‚≠ê1) - Minimal theme, includes git status decorations.
  • unit-1 (‚≠ê0) - Minimalist theme with ITWTB colors.
  • vercel (‚≠ê191) - Minimalist theme with git status decorations.
  • vertepommes (‚≠ê0) - Based on ys. Includes vcs status, username and current directory decorations.
  • vitesse (‚≠ê1) - Inspired by VS Code's Vitesse (‚≠ê621) theme. Includes git status decorations.
  • vulcan (‚≠ê0) - Minimal theme reminiscent of the default bash theme. Includes git decorations.
  • wade (‚≠ê5) - Mashup of the popular ZSH themes Agnoster and Fishy (‚≠ê180k), with some visual tweaks.
  • wang-iterm (‚≠ê5) - Based on the 0532 theme.
  • whale (‚≠ê2) - Fast reimplementation of the whale theme.
  • whales (‚≠ê0) - Includes decorators for git status, java version, last command return status, and directory.
  • wild-cherry (‚≠ê481) - A fairy-tale inspired theme for ZSH, iTerm 2, Sublime, Atom, & Mou.
  • wkentaro (‚≠ê1) - A simple theme for Python users. Includes virtualenv and git status decorators.
  • work-line (‚≠ê6) - Theme with nice emojis.
  • workbench (‚≠ê4) - Includes git status decorations, working directory, exit status of last command and current virtualenv.
  • xavi (‚≠ê0) - Modified version of the gnzh (‚≠ê180k) theme with emoji decorations for git status and current directory.
  • xlk-simple (‚≠ê1) - Simple theme with git decorations.
  • xm (‚≠ê0) - Theme for dark terminals. Has git decorations.
  • xor (‚≠ê1) - Self described as minimalistic and 'feature-poor', includes git decorations.
  • xremix (‚≠ê1) - An oh-my-zsh shell theme based on the Jreese theme plugin.
  • xris47 (‚≠ê1) - Fast, simple and streamlined theme. Works best with tmux (‚≠ê38k) and vim-airline (‚≠ê18k).
  • yairshefi (‚≠ê1) - Minimal theme with line separated prompts. Based on the robbyrussell (‚≠ê180k) theme.
  • yazpt (‚≠ê7) - A clean, fast, good-looking ZSH prompt theme that thoughtfully incorporates Git/Subversion/TFVC status info, integrates with popular plugin managers like Oh My Zsh, and is straightforward to customize and extend.
  • yechen (‚≠ê0) - Minimalist theme with git status decorations.
  • yeet (‚≠ê0) - Minimalist prompt with git status decorations.
  • yindev (‚≠ê2) - Variant of gndx. Includes decorations for git status and current directory.
  • ykmam (‚≠ê1) - Modified from ys (‚≠ê0) theme and optimized for a dark background.
  • ysm (‚≠ê1) - Simple ZSH theme with git status information.
  • yuki (‚≠ê6) - A dark optimized ZSH theme.
  • yyl-ys (‚≠ê38) - Includes conda and venv status.
  • yz50 (‚≠ê1) - Colorful, based off of robbyrussell (‚≠ê180k) and crunch (‚≠ê180k) themes. Includes git status decorations.
  • z4rr3t (‚≠ê1) - Based on sindresorhus' pure (‚≠ê14k) theme.
  • zemm-blinks (‚≠ê7) - Customized version of oh-my-zsh blinks (‚≠ê180k) with mercurial support and other changes.
  • zemoji (‚≠ê5) - Based on wild-cherry (‚≠ê481). Includes exit status, virtualenv, nvm, rvm and git status decorations.
  • zeroastro (‚≠ê7) - Works best on dark backgrounds, includes git status decorations.
  • zerocake (‚≠ê0) - Works better on dark brackgrounds.
  • zest (‚≠ê0) - A functional theme for ZSH. Influenced by zsh2000 (‚≠ê106), agnoster and powerline (‚≠ê1.2k) themes.
  • zlambda (‚≠ê0) - Minimalist, includes git decorations without special font requirements.
  • zodiac (‚≠ê0) - Includes an emoji for the animal corresponding to the current year.
  • zprompts (‚≠ê6) - Themes (prompts) that use original zsh theming subsystem.
  • zqt (‚≠ê3) - Modified version of oh-my-zsh's maran (‚≠ê180k) theme.

  • zsh313 (‚≠ê0) - Minimal theme with git status decorations.
  • zshpower (‚≠ê14) - Optimized for python developers. Includes git and pyenv status decorations, username and host. Tries to install other plugins and fonts, so read its instructions before installing.
  • zshred (‚≠ê1) - Shows current directory, git decorations, exit status of last command and time.
  • zwsh (‚≠ê0) - A Zpm3/Wordstar mode/theme for ZSH.
  • zys (‚≠ê10) - Similar to Agnoster (‚≠ê4.1k), designed to disclose information contextually, with a powerline aesthetic.
  • zzshell (‚≠ê0) - Inspired by the default Oh-My-Zsh theme. Displays exit code and git status decorations. Doesn't require Powerline fonts.

Nov 15 - Nov 21, 2021

Generic ZSH

  • ZSH Unplugged (‚≠ê443) - Good resource if you want to eliminate using a framework but still easily use plugins.

Oct 25 - Oct 31, 2021

Zinit

  • Turbo mode ‚Äì 80% faster ZSH startup! for example: instead of 200 ms, it'll be 40 ms
  • Completion management (selectively disable and enable completions)
  • Snippets (‚Üî regular files downloaded via-URL, e.g.: scripts) and through them Oh My Zsh and Prezto plugins support (‚Üí low overhead)
  • Annexes (‚Üî Zinit extensions)
  • Reports (from the plugin loads ‚Äì plugins are no longer black boxes)
  • Plugin unloading (allows e.g.: dynamic theme switching)
  • bindkey capturing and remapping
  • packages
  • Clean fpath (the array $fpath is not being used to add completions and autoload functions, hence it stays concise, not bloated)
  • Services ‚Üî a single-instance, background plugins
  • Also, in general: all the mechanisms from the ZSH Plugin Standard ‚Äì Zinit is a reference implementation of the standard.

Other References / superconsole - Windows-only

  • Mastering ZSH (‚≠ê1.5k) is a great tutorial that builds on the basics to show you advanced ZSH usage, customizations, and practical examples.

Feb 01 - Feb 07, 2021

znap

  • Multi-repo management
  • Automatic compinit and bashinit - you no longer need them in your .zshrc, znap will do them automatically as needed.

zinit

  • 1.9k+ aliases
  • 330+ git aliases
  • 2.8k line README.md

Sep 28 - Oct 04, 2020

znap

  • Make any prompt appear instantly. Reduce your startup time from ~200ms to ~40ms with just one command.
  • Asynchronously compile your plugins and functions.
  • Cache those expensive eval $(commands).
  • Clone or pull multiple repos in parallel.
  • Re-clone all your repos without you having to re-enter them.

Sep 07 - Sep 13, 2020

zinit

  • 1 line install

Aug 27 - Sep 02, 2018

zplug

  • Can manage everything
    • ZSH plugins/UNIX commands on GitHub and Bitbucket
    • Gist files (gist.github.com)
    • Externally managed plugins e.g., oh-my-zsh (‚≠ê180k) and prezto (‚≠ê14k) plugins/themes
    • Binary artifacts on GitHub Releases
    • Local plugins
    • etc. (you can add your own sources (‚≠ê5.9k)!)
  • Super-fast parallel installation/update
  • Support for lazy-loading
  • Branch/tag/commit support
  • Post-update, post-load hooks
  • Interactive interface (fzf (‚≠ê72k), peco (‚≠ê7.8k), zaw (‚≠ê577), and so on)
  • Cache mechanism for reducing the startup time (‚≠ê5.9k)
